# Seshat BI -- Idea Bank

> **This is a future-idea bank, not a roadmap and not a commitment.** Nothing here is
> planned, scheduled, or approved. It is exploratory brainstorming output to browse for
> inspiration. The authoritative roadmap is `docs/roadmap/roadmap.md` (F-numbered features).

_Re-running regenerates this file as a HISTORY-AWARE snapshot: each run still re-reasons every
_idea from scratch, but it now READS the prior bank and Ground's verified ship-status first, so
_an idea that has since SHIPPED is recorded as shipped (with its evidence) and a settled rejection
_is not re-litigated. This is still an idea BANK, not an evolving plan: nothing here is promoted,
_scheduled, or committed. A SHIPPED tag only records that a human already took an equivalent idea
_through the normal feature process -- the engine never moves an idea onto the roadmap itself. The
_verdicts and scores are an automated reviewer's triage opinion. An idea advances only through the
_normal spec/feature process, with a human decision._

_Generated by the `idea-engine` workflow. Generated on 2026-07-01._

> **DEGRADED RUN: adversarial skeptic did not challenge 18 candidate(s) -- those were clamped (killed, demoted from ADOPT) for unproven coverage. Treat this bank as partial.**

**52 ideas scored** (generated across 3 rounds; raw pre-dedupe 81; 10 near-duplicate entries merged). Verdicts: ADOPT 14, CONSIDER 34, PARK 4, REJECT 0. Horizon: NOW 35, HORIZON 17.

## Reviewer portfolio verdict

> The panel evaluated ~40 candidate ideas and cleanly separated a build-now tier from a hold tier. Highest-conviction ADOPTs with no eligibility doubt: E6 (rule-scaffold generator + doctor), G1 (design-foundation idea lane), E4 (adversarial fixture corpus + golden-findings lock), E1 (5-place wiring meta-gate), F4 (rule-count claim reconciler), H1 (additivity-consistency lineage), and J1 (approval evidence pack) -- all governance/lint/evidence seams that make the design and rule layers machine-checkable without executing anything. Several top-value ideas (A1 token->theme reconciler at 9/9, C1 design-review evidence gate, B1 anti-pattern parity, A3 WCAG contrast) score as ADOPT-grade but carry an eligibility SPLIT: reviewers scored them high, yet the hard-principle auditor kept a flag over read-only vs decision-resolving boundaries or APPROVE-adjacency, landing them at CONSIDER pending a tight scope statement. Two ideas need engineering fixes before they pay off: B1's extractor is confirmed broken (needs two extractors -- ### headings vs a pipe table), and E3's coverage proof is blocked until B1's hardcoded module list becomes introspectable. The clearest hold is H5 (exception-watchlist), the sole idea two reviewers ruled INELIGIBLE for smuggling threshold semantics into the settled F5/F6 stats-engine rejection zone -- PARK it unless reframed as strict presence/absence. Other PARKs (A10 provenance lint, E5 severity contract, I4 namespace lint, H11 answerability digest) are low value/feasibility, not principle problems. Recommended action: ship the seven clean ADOPTs first, resolve the SPLIT scope questions on A1/C1/A3/A11/D2/F3/H8/H9 with a one-line eligibility clarification per idea, fix B1's extractor before wiring it, and defer H5."

## Legend

- **Verdict** (reviewer's *triage opinion only* -- not a decision to build) -- ADOPT (worth a closer look first; eligible, consistent, high value) - CONSIDER (interesting; needs a decision or dependency) - PARK (horizon / later) - REJECT (ineligible or conflicts -- kept for the record).
- **Horizon** -- `NOW` (fits the repo today) - `HORIZON` (future vision).
- **Eligibility** -- respects all hard principles, or violates one (named in the rationale).
- **V / F** -- value / feasibility (1-10), reviewer-assigned.
- **SHIPPED / SETTLED** -- a prior idea Memory matched to shipped work or a settled rejection; kept for the record, not an open candidate.

## ADOPT

### A2. Theme JSON Token-Contract / Four-Surface Purity Linter

`NOW` - **V7 / F8** - consistency: consistent - respects principles

**Why this verdict:** [HARD-PRINCIPLE AUDITOR -- I judge ELIGIBILITY only and presume each idea ineligible until it proves it touches ONLY reasoning/static/read-only seams. I name the violated principle for anything that executes, self-grants/bypasses a gate, fabricates confidence, resolves an ambiguity a human owns, or is C086-specific. I verified the four load-bearing facts myself: (1) validate_cards.py is stdlib-only (re/sys/pathlib), parses text, never renders -- D2 clears never-execute; (2) severity_posture.py's ratified 044 docstring states severity is OBSERVED per-branch, NOT a rule property (one id emits a SET), and the module itself uses subprocess to force rules -- so E2/E5's 'declare severity on @register / a governed per-rule severity table' sub-claims are architecturally ineligible-as-framed; (3) B1 hardcodes its governed-module list (never_execute.py lines 66-68), it does NOT glob, so E3's introspectable-selection dependency is real (HORIZON-gated, not disqualifying); (4) A1's token->theme hex drift is real and A1/A5/pbir all stay strictly read-only (pbir.py reads .Report and never writes). My eligibility verdicts: I mark ELIGIBLE the static-CHECK / pure-DEFINE / read-only-aggregator ideas that never author PBIP/PBIR, never run DAX, never compute a confidence score, and never write approvals[]. I flag as ineligible (named principle) ONLY sub-claims that genuinely cross a line: E2 and E5's severity-collapse sub-part conflicts with the ratified observed-not-declared model (I keep the parent ideas eligible on their surviving two-thirds but mark them minor-tension). H5 is the sole idea I hold on the settled-rejection line: its human-declared bands still smuggle threshold semantics into the settled F5/F6 stats-engine rejection zone; eligible-in-principle only if strictly presence/absence, so I PARK it as relitigation-risk. Everything computing WCAG contrast (A3/A4) I judged carefully: deterministic sRGB arithmetic from committed static hexes against a token-declared floor is a pass/fail categorical test, NOT a fabricated confidence score and NOT rendered-pixel execution -- eligible. Every APPROVE-adjacent idea (C1, H8, J1) I confirmed is structurally verify-slot-only with an empty approvals[] the human signs -- eligible because it packages, never grants. No idea is C086-bound: the c086 report is cited as one worked-example corpus a generic glob reads, not hardcoded (A5/A8 reuse pbir's is_test_path exemption). Default posture: strict, but the set was pre-filtered and pre-differentiated, so most survive the eligibility gate; my value is naming the two severity sub-claims and the one relitigation case the other reviewers may wave through.] Structural key-presence/absence scan over theme JSON against the surface-3 MAY/MUST-NOT contract. For the analytical/KPI (H), routing (F), engine-wiring (E), cross-layer (I), approve-support (J), observability (K) themes that sit outside my design expertise, I defer -- scoring conservatively and flagging that these are not my lane rather than distorting the panel.] The underlying design concern is one I strongly hold: a soft readability heuristic (hierarchy/grid-fit) must NEVER hard-gate a stage the way a purity contamination must -- the visual-qa 'warning != stage fail' split is load-bearing (I re-read it: nine style findings are warning-class, four are blocked). But the skeptic found the framing fights the ratified 044 architecture: severity is OBSERVED per-branch, not declared per-rule, so 'a governed severity table keyed per D-rule' is weakened. The valid concern can be honored by which BRANCH emits which severity. Engine-governance, partly outside my lane -- moderate confidence.

**First step:** Honor the concern at the branch level: ensure each D-rule's readability findings emit warning-severity and its purity/fidelity findings emit error, then let severity-posture observe it; skip the per-rule declared table.

## Rescue notes (steelman of the not-adopted)

_A reframing that MIGHT make an idea eligible later, or the irreducible reason it stays out. A reason for a human to weigh next run -- never a verdict; the gate already ruled._

- **A1. Token->Theme Compile Reconciler** -- rescue possible. Ship it as the FIRST rule of a net-new design-lint family under src/retail/rules/ (verified greenfield). Read-only YAML+JSON field-compare over the DECLARED compiles_to relationship (tokens line 69), catching a currently-RED drift on day one. It reports a Finding, never authors the theme, never resolves which side is canonical. Narrowed seam: Scope v1 to ONLY the fields tokens explicitly declares as compiled (primary + the sentiment success/warning/danger triple), not the whole dataColors ordering, so the rule has an unambiguous declared source-of-truth and cannot be accused of inventing a mapping.
- **A3. WCAG Contrast Pre-Check (from static hex tokens)** -- rescue possible. Frame as a categorical pass/fail regression-GUARD against owner-declared WCAG floors (4.5:1/3:1), computed by deterministic stdlib sRGB arithmetic over committed hexes. It compares to a named floor the owner set -- not a fabricated confidence score. Output is 'pair X below its declared floor', nothing rendered, nothing authored. Narrowed seam: Narrow v1 to only the specific foreground/background token PAIRS the design foundation explicitly declares as text-on-surface (not every color combination), so the floor for each pair is owner-declared rather than guessed by the rule.
- **A10. Surface-Stamp Provenance Lint** -- rescue possible. Drop the stamp schema; re-pitch as a read-only coverage AUDIT that asserts A2+A8 collectively cover every template surface -- a guard-the-guards check over EXISTING contracts, adding no schema field and no forbidden-token guess-list. Narrowed seam: Instead of authoring a `surface:` schema field across all templates, glob the template set and assert each template is claimed by exactly one existing purity contract (A2 or A8), reporting any un-covered template as a Finding -- zero new authored surface, zero guess-list.
- **A11. Presentation-Format Reconciler** -- rescue possible. The SECOND always-safe reconciler in the A1 family -- a DISTINCT pair (tokens.number_format -> visual-spec consumer). Reuses the template's existing override_reason field (no schema invention), read-only, categorical, no-op until specs are filled. Enforces the declared token-reuse promise / anti-pattern #4. Narrowed seam: Gate the rule to fire only on visual-specs that HAVE a filled number_format, and require override_reason only on a genuine divergence -- so on an empty corpus it is a silent no-op, and it never demands content that does not exist yet.
- **B1. Anti-Pattern Parity Rule (workflow<->prose thirteen-in-lockstep)** -- rescue possible. Adopt the intent with the CORRECTED shape: a prose<->prose set-equality reconcile of the 13 anti-patterns, distinct from shipped SC1 (status<->file). Enforces the docs' explicit 'keep the two in sync' instruction that nothing currently guards. Narrowed seam: Build TWO format-specific extractors, not one: dashboard-qa.md stores the 13 as a Markdown pipe table (| # | Anti-pattern |) while visual-qa.md uses '### N.' headings (I confirmed both formats). The single-extractor rough_shape is a verified no-op on one file; the narrowed, buildable seam is 'two extractors -> one set-compare'.
- **C1. Screenshot-QA / Design-Review Evidence Schema + Static Completeness Gate** -- rescue possible. A committed design-review evidence schema (anti-patterns keyed to B1's 13, human-entered contrast pairs, findings, reviewer/date) PLUS a verify-slot-only completeness rule. Fills the verified prose-only-evidence gap; checks the slot conforms, never makes the judgment, never self-grants dashboard_ready. Narrowed seam: The schema IS the deliverable (no missing content dependency); keep contrast_pairs as human-entered FACTS, not computed, so the rule stays strictly presence/conformance and never fabricates a score. Build C1 first, then H8 extends its spine.
- **D2. Adopt orphaned validate_cards.py into the governed check surface** -- rescue possible. Pure adoption of a verified working orphan (validate_cards.py, stdlib-only, parses text, never renders) into a governed pytest case + count anchor. Reuses the checker verbatim; fills the brand-half enforcement gap no other idea covers. Low effort, gated on nothing. Narrowed seam: Narrow the deliverable to exactly two artifacts: a pytest case running its existing main() over the committed card bundle, plus a count anchor for the bundle size -- reusing the checker verbatim, adding almost no code.
- **E3. Never-Execute Self-Audit (prove B1/B3 cover every rule module)** -- rescue possible. Re-pitch with a corrected, narrower premise: never_execute.py ALREADY globs the rules package via _GOVERNED_PREFIX, so new D-rule modules are covered. The real residual seam is only the 4 hardcoded core modules (cli/runner/core/registry) -- a small exhaustiveness assertion over a finite set, not a sweeping guard-the-guard. Narrowed seam: A read-only ast/glob reconcile that asserts (a) the prefix still resolves to the rules package and (b) the 4 explicitly-listed core modules still exist and are the complete import-chain root set -- flagging drift if a new non-rules core module is added without being governed.
- **E5. Design-Lint Severity Contract** -- rescue possible. Drop the per-rule severity TABLE. Honor the real concern (soft heuristic must not hard-gate) in the ratified model's terms: encode it as each D-rule's BRANCH design -- which branch emits WARNING vs ERROR -- observed via the existing severity-posture, adding no declared contract. Narrowed seam: Fold the intent into each D-rule as a branch-design requirement + a severity-posture golden fixture that OBSERVES the emitted set, rather than a governed table declaring severity per rule.
- **E7. retail doctor -- Proactive Lockstep-Drift Diagnostician (read, never fix)** -- rescue possible. Strictly a read-only aggregating HELPER: one comprehensive read across all known drift classes, emitting status + evidence + blocking_reasons with no score. Wraps and concatenates the individual reconcilers' Findings -- never a gate, never a second source of truth. Distinct from K1. Narrowed seam: Bind it to be a convenience wrapper that CALLS the individual reconciler rules and concatenates their existing Findings -- never a gate, never a second source of truth, never mutating or scoring -- so all enforcement stays in the individual rules.
- **F3. Shipped-Ledger Reconciler (backlog appendix <-> shipped-ideas.yaml)** -- rescue possible. A currently-RED bijection reconcile: backlog appendix vs shipped-ideas.yaml diverge today (only 2 of 7 kraken ids in the appendix). Reuses shipped A3 bijection posture + stdlib id extractor; read-only, categorical; locks provenance of shipped work. Both gold sources exist now. Narrowed seam: Scope v1 to a pure id-set bijection over the two ledgers (yaml ids <-> prose-appendix ids extracted by a stdlib regex), reporting missing/extra ids -- not reconciling any richer metadata, so the gold source (both files) fully exists today.
- **H5. Exception-Watchlist Contract Family** -- rescue possible. Only admissible as a strictly presence/absence, observed-only contract with ZERO band/threshold vocabulary -- define that a human-entered exception note exists (yes/no), never 'high/normal/low' bands or a stockout cutoff, which would re-enter the settled F5/F6 zone. Narrowed seam: Strip it to a pure DEFINE-of-slot + presence CHECK (does a human-authored exception note exist for this metric, yes/no) with no computed comparison and no band vocabulary anywhere in the schema or the rule.
- **H8. KPI-Sufficiency Signal in the Dashboard-Ready Evidence Spine** -- rescue possible. A design<->KPI bridge on the readiness spine that SURFACES an existing metric-contract's sufficiency as a blocking_reason INPUT -- human still approves, never self-grants dashboard_ready, never invents a metric. Build as an extension of C1's schema, sequenced after H4 lands. Narrowed seam: Narrow to reading H4's sufficiency card and emitting it as one more blocking_reason on the existing readiness spine -- no new judgment, no computation -- and build it as an EXTENSION of C1's evidence schema.
- **H9. Land Planned Time-Intelligence + Same-Store Contracts** -- rescue possible. Honest CONTENT completion, not a governance seam: DEFINE-only additivity/grain contracts for the highest-frequency finance asks (YTD/MTD, PoP, same-store), filling a verified [planned] gap. No DAX, no computation; records the marked-date-table dependency as a blocking_reason. It is the content half H6 checks and unblocks H6/H7. Narrowed seam: Scope each contract to additivity/grain semantics only (semi-additive cumulative caveat, non-additive growth, required marked-date-table recorded as a blocking_reason) -- pure DEFINE, no generated measure, no threshold.
- **I4. Metric-Contract Namespace Disambiguation Lint** -- rescue possible. Drop the mandated marker; re-pitch as a read-only DETECT-and-report lint that merely surfaces the verified three-way naming collision as an informational Finding, imposing no schema change on the three mature families. Preserves the seam, removes the churn. Narrowed seam: Detect-and-report only: glob the three families, flag the colliding term, and point to the existing INDEX prose that already disambiguates -- never require a new marker field, so mature surfaces are untouched.
